-- Create 3 tables. Each should have a primary key, and a foreign key that references one of your other tables' primary key. Each should have 4 columns. -- Use 4 different data types. Use at least 2 kinds of constraint besides primary and foreign keys. Use at least 1 default value. CREATE TABLE books ( book_Id NUMBER(7) CONSTRAINT book_id_pk PRIMARY KEY, book_title VARCHAR2(20), author VARCHAR2(20) DEFAULT 'Robert Villium', price NUMBER(8,2) ) CREATE TABLE library_member ( member_id Number(7) CONSTRAINT member_id_pk Primary Key, name VARCHAR2(20), address VARCHAR2(20), dob DATE ) CREATE TABLE loan_info ( loan_info_id NUMBER(7) CONSTRAINT loan_info_id_pk Primary Key, member NUMBER(7) CONSTRAINT member_fk REFERENCES library_member(member_id), book NUMBER(7) CONSTRAINT book_fk REFERENCES books(book_id), borrow_date DATE, returned CHAR(5) )
"ORA-00900: invalid SQL statement"
